    SELECT TOP(1) [s].[Id], [s].[AppUserId], [s].[CategoryId], [s].[CompleteDate], [s].[CreateDate], [s].[Description], [s].[IsComplete], [s].[Title], [a].[Id] AS [Id0], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate0], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[Name], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[Surname], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName], [c].[Id] AS [Id1], [c].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate1], [c].[Name] AS [Name0]
    FROM [ShoppingLists] AS [s]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a] ON [s].[AppUserId] = [a].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [s].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
    WHERE [s].[Id] = @__request_Id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [Products] AS [p] ON [t].[Id] = [p].[ShoppingListId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t].[Id1]
